> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-396">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-396">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-397">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-397">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-398">Per la registrazione di routine in un'app ASP.NET Core, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-398">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-399">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-399">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-400">Risolvere i problemi in IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-400">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-401">Registro eventi applicazioni (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-401">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-402">Accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-402">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-403">Aprire il menu Start, cercare *Visualizzatore eventi*e selezionare l'app **Visualizzatore eventi.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-403">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-404">In **Visualizzatore eventi** aprire il nodo **Registri di Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-404">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-405">Selezionare **Applicazione** per aprire il log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-405">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-406">Cercare gli errori associati all'app in cui si è verificato il problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-406">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-407">Gli errori presentano un valore *Modulo AspNetCore IIS* o *Modulo AspNetCore IIS Express* nella colonna *Origine*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-407">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-408">Eseguire l'app da un prompt dei comandi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-408">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-409">Molti errori di avvio non producono informazioni utili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-409">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-410">È possibile individuare la causa di alcuni errori eseguendo l'app da un prompt dei comandi nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-410">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-411">Distribuzione dipendente dal framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-411">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-412">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-412">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-413">Da un prompt dei comandi passare alla cartella di distribuzione e avviare l'app eseguendo l'assembly dell'app con *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-413">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-414">Nel comando seguente sostituire \<assembly_name> con il nome dell'assembly dell'app: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-414">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-415">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà scritto nella finestra della console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-415">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-416">Se gli errori si verificano quando si effettua una richiesta all'app, effettuare una richiesta all'host e alla porta su cui è in ascolto Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-416">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-417">Usando l'host e la porta predefiniti, effettuare una richiesta a `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-417">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-418">Se l'app risponde normalmente nell'indirizzo endpoint di Kestrel, è più probabile che il problema sia associato alla configurazione dell'host e che non sia interno all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-418">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-419">Distribuzione autonoma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-419">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-420">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-420">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-421">Da un prompt dei comandi passare alla cartella di distribuzione e avviare il file eseguibile dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-421">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-422">Nel comando seguente sostituire \<assembly_name> con il nome dell'assembly dell'app: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-422">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-423">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà scritto nella finestra della console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-423">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-424">Se gli errori si verificano quando si effettua una richiesta all'app, effettuare una richiesta all'host e alla porta su cui è in ascolto Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-424">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-425">Usando l'host e la porta predefiniti, effettuare una richiesta a `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-425">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-426">Se l'app risponde normalmente nell'indirizzo endpoint di Kestrel, è più probabile che il problema sia associato alla configurazione dell'host e che non sia interno all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-426">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-427">ASP.NET registro stdout del modulo principale (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-427">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-428">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-428">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-429">Passare alla cartella di distribuzione del sito nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-429">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-430">Se la cartella *logs* non è presente, creare la cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-430">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-431">Per istruzioni su come impostare MSBuild per la creazione automatica della cartella *logs* nella distribuzione, vedere l'argomento [Struttura della directory](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-431">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-432">Modificare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-432">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-433">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e modificare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in modo da fare riferimento alla cartella *logs*, ad esempio `.\logs\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-433">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-434">`stdout` nel percorso è il prefisso del nome del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-434">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-435">Un timestamp, l'ID del processo e l'estensione del file vengono aggiunti automaticamente al momento della creazione del log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-435">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-436">Usando `stdout` come prefisso del nome del file, un tipico file di log è denominato *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-436">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-437">Assicurarsi che l'identità del pool di applicazioni disponga delle autorizzazioni di scrittura per la cartella *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-437">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-438">Salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-438">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-439">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-439">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-440">Passare alla cartella *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-440">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-441">Trovare e aprire il log stdout più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-441">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-442">Esaminare il log per verificare se sono presenti errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-442">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-443">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-443">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-444">Modificare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-444">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-445">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-445">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-446">Salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-446">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-447">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-447">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-448">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-448">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-449">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-449">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-450">Per la registrazione di routine in un'app ASP.NET Core, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-450">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-451">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-451">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-452">ASP.NET registro di debug del modulo principale (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-452">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-453">Aggiungi le seguenti impostazioni del gestore al file *web.config* dell'app per abilitare ASP.NET log di debug del modulo principale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-453">Add the following handler settings to the app's *web.config* file to enable ASP.NET Core Module debug log:</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore ...>
  <handlerSettings>
    <handlerSetting name="debugLevel" value="file" />
    <handlerSetting name="debugFile" value="c:\temp\ancm.log" />
  </handlerSettings>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-454">Verificare che il percorso specificato per il log esista e che l'identità del pool di applicazioni abbia le autorizzazioni di scrittura nel percorso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-454">Confirm that the path specified for the log exists and that the app pool's identity has write permissions to the location.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-455">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-455">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-456">Abilitare la pagina delle eccezioni per gli sviluppatori</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-456">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-457">La variabile di ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [ può essere aggiunta a web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) per eseguire l'app nell'ambiente di sviluppo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-457">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-458">Purché l'ambiente non sia sottoposto a override durante l'avvio dell'app tramite `UseEnvironment` nel generatore di host, l'impostazione della variabile di ambiente consente di visualizzare la [pagina delle eccezioni per gli sviluppatori](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) quando viene eseguita l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-458">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout"
      hostingModel="InProcess">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-459">L'impostazione della variabile di ambiente per `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` è consigliata solo per l'uso in server di gestione temporanea e test non esposti a Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-459">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-460">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, rimuovere la variabile di ambiente dal file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-460">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-461">Per informazioni sull'impostazione delle variabili di ambiente in *web.config*, vedere [elemento figlio environmentVariables di aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-461">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-462">Ottenere dati da un'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-462">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-463">Se un'app è in grado di rispondere alle richieste, è possibile ottenere dati sulle richieste, le connessioni e altri dati dall'app tramite middleware inline di terminale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-463">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-464">Per altre informazioni e codice di esempio, vedere <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-464">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-465">App lenta o sospesa (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-465">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-466">Un dump di *arresto anomalo* del sistema è uno snapshot della memoria del sistema e consente di determinare la causa di un arresto anomalo dell'app, un errore di avvio o un'app lenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-466">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-467">Arresto anomalo o eccezione di un'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-467">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-468">Ottenere e analizzare un dump da [Segnalazione errori Windows](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-468">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-469">Creare una cartella per i file dump di arresto anomalo del sistema in `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-469">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-470">Il pool di app deve avere accesso in scrittura alla cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-470">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-471">Eseguire lo [script di PowerShell EnableDumps](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-471">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-472">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting in-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-472">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-473">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-473">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-474">Eseguire l'app nelle condizioni che causano l'arresto anomalo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-474">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-475">Dopo che si è verificato l'arresto anomalo, eseguire lo [script di PowerShell DisableDumps](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-475">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-476">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting in-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-476">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-477">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-477">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-478">Dopo l'arresto anomalo di un'app e la raccolta dei dump, l'app può terminare normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-478">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-479">Lo script di PowerShell configura Segnalazione errori Windows per raccogliere fino a cinque dump per ogni app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-479">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-480">I dump di arresto anomalo del sistema potrebbero richiedere una grande quantità di spazio su disco (fino a diversi gigabyte ognuno).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-480">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-481">L'app si blocca, si verifica un errore durante l'avvio o viene eseguita normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-481">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-482">Quando un'app *si blocca* (si blocca ma non si arresta in modo anomalo), non riesce durante l'avvio o viene eseguito normalmente, vedere File di dump in [modalità utente: Scelta dello strumento migliore](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) per selezionare uno strumento appropriato per produrre il dump.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-482">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-483">Analizzare il dump</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-483">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-484">È possibile analizzare un dump usando diversi approcci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-484">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-485">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file) (Analisi di un file dump in modalità utente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-485">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-486">Cancellare le cache dei pacchetti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-486">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-487">Un'app funzionante potrebbe non riuscire immediatamente dopo l'aggiornamento di .NET Core SDK nel computer di sviluppo o la modifica delle versioni del pacchetto all'interno dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-487">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-488">In alcuni casi i pacchetti incoerenti possono interrompere un'app quando si eseguono aggiornamenti principali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-488">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-489">La maggior parte di questi problemi può essere risolta attenendosi alle istruzioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-489">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-490">Eliminare le cartelle *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-490">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-491">Cancellare le cache dei pacchetti eseguendo [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) da una shell dei comandi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-491">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-492">La cancellazione delle cache dei pacchetti può essere eseguita anche `nuget locals all -clear`con lo strumento [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e l'esecuzione del comando .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-492">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-493">*nuget.exe* non è un'installazione inclusa con il sistema operativo desktop Windows e deve essere ottenuta separatamente dal [sito Web NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-493">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-494">Ripristinare e ricompilare il progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-494">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-495">Eliminare tutti i file nella cartella di distribuzione nel server prima di ridistribuire l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-495">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-526">Errori di avvio delle app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-526">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-527">In Visual Studio, per impostazione predefinita un progetto ASP.NET Core usa l'hosting in [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) durante il debug.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-527">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-528">A *502.5 - Errore* di processo o *500.30 - Errore di avvio* che si verifica durante il debug locale può essere diagnosticato utilizzando i suggerimenti in questo argomento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-528">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-529">403.14 Vietato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-529">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-530">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-530">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-531">Viene registrato il seguente errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-531">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-532">L'errore è in genere causato da una distribuzione interrotta nel sistema di hosting, che include uno dei seguenti scenari:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-532">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-533">L'app viene distribuita nella cartella errata nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-533">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-534">Il processo di distribuzione non è riuscito a spostare tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app nella cartella di distribuzione nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-534">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-535">Il file *web.config* non è presente nella distribuzione oppure il formato del file *web.config* non è corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-535">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-536">Eseguire la procedura seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-536">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-537">Eliminare tutti i file e le cartelle dalla cartella di distribuzione nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-537">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-538">Ridistribuire il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* dell'app nel sistema di hosting usando il normale metodo di distribuzione, ad esempio Visual Studio, PowerShell o distribuzione manuale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-538">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-539">Verificare che il file *web.config* sia presente nella distribuzione e che il relativo contenuto sia corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-539">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-540">Quando si esegue l'hosting nel servizio app `D:\home\site\wwwroot` di Azure, verificare che l'app sia distribuita nella cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-540">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-541">Quando l'app è ospitata da IIS, verificare che l'app sia distribuita nel **percorso fisico** di IIS visualizzato nelle **impostazioni**di base di **Gestione IIS.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-541">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-542">Verificare che tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app vengano distribuiti confrontando la distribuzione nel sistema di hosting con il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* del progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-542">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-543">Per ulteriori informazioni sul layout di un'app ASP.NET Core pubblicata, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-543">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-544">Per ulteriori informazioni sul file *web.config,* vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-544">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-545">500 - Errore interno del server</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-545">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-546">L'app viene avviata, ma un errore impedisce al server di soddisfare la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-546">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-547">Questo errore si verifica all'interno del codice dell'app durante l'avvio o durante la creazione di una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-547">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-548">La risposta potrebbe non avere alcun contenuto o essere visualizzata nel browser come un codice *500 Errore interno del server*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-548">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-549">Il log eventi dell'applicazione in genere indica che l'app è stata avviata normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-549">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-550">Dal punto di vista del server, questo è corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-550">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-551">L'app è stata effettivamente avviata, ma non può generare una risposta valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-551">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-552">Per risolvere il problema, eseguire l'app dal prompt dei comandi nel server o abilitare il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-552">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-553">500.0 Errore di caricamento del gestore in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-553">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-554">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-554">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-555">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-555">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-556">Il [modulo di base ASP.NET](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) non riesce a trovare CLR .NET Core e al gestore richieste in-process (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-556">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the .NET Core CLR and find the in-process request handler (*aspnetcorev2_inprocess.dll*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-557">Controllare che:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-557">Check that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-558">L'app specifichi come destinazione il pacchetto NuGet [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) o il [metapacchetto Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-558">The app targets either the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS](https://www.nuget.org/packages/Microsoft.AspNetCore.Server.IIS) NuGet package or the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-559">Le versione del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core specificata come destinazione dall'app sia installata nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-559">The version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that the app targets is installed on the target machine.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-560">500.0 Errore di caricamento del gestore out-of-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-560">500.0 Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-561">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-561">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-562">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-562">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-563">[L'ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) non riesce a trovare il gestore di richiesta di hosting out-of-process.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-563">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) fails to find the out-of-process hosting request handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-564">Verificare che *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* sia presente in una sottocartella accanto ad *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-564">Make sure the *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll* is present in a subfolder next to *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-565">502.5 Errore del processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-565">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-566">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-566">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-567">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-567">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-568">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta di avviare il processo di lavoro, ma l'avvio non riesce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-568">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-569">In genere è possibile determinare la causa di un errore di avvio del processo dalle voci nel log eventi dell'applicazione e nel log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-569">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-570">Una condizione di errore comune è dovuta alla configurazione non corretta dell'app perché come destinazione viene specificata una versione del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core, che non è presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-570">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-571">Controllare le versioni del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core installate nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-571">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-572">Il *framework condiviso* è il set di assembly (file *DLL*) che vengono installati nel computer e cui fa riferimento un metapacchetto, ad esempio `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-572">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-573">Il riferimento del metapacchetto può specificare una versione minima richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-573">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-574">Per altre informazioni, vedere [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/) (Il framework condiviso).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-574">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-575">La pagina di errore *502.5 Errore del processo* viene restituita quando il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo a causa di un errore di configurazione dell'hosting o dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-575">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-576">Non è stato possibile avviare l'aggiornamento dell'applicazione. Errore: 0x800700c1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-576">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-577">L'app non è stata avviata perché non è stato possibile caricarne l'assembly (*.dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-577">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-578">Questo errore si verifica quando è presente una mancata corrispondenza del numero di bit tra l'app pubblicata e il processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-578">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-579">Verificare che l'impostazione del pool di app a 32 bit sia corretta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-579">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-580">Selezionare il pool di app in **Pool di applicazioni** di Gestione IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-580">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-581">Selezionare **Impostazioni avanzate** in **Modifica pool di applicazioni** nel pannello **Azioni**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-581">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-582">Impostare **Attiva applicazioni a 32 bit**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-582">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-583">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 32 bit (x86), impostare il valore su `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-583">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-584">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 64 bit (x64), impostare il valore su `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-584">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-585">Verificare che non vi sia `<Platform>` un conflitto tra una proprietà MSBuild nel file di progetto e il numero di bit pubblicato dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-585">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-586">Reimpostazione della connessione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-586">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-587">Se si verifica un errore dopo l'invio delle intestazioni, è troppo tardi perché il server possa inviare un codice **500 Errore interno del server** quando si verifica un errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-587">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-588">Questo spesso accade quando si verifica un errore durante la serializzazione di oggetti complessi per una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-588">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-589">Questo tipo di errore viene visualizzato come un errore di *reimpostazione della connessione* nel client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-589">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-590">La [registrazione delle applicazioni](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) può consentire di risolvere questi tipi di errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-590">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-591">Limiti di avvio predefiniti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-591">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-592">Il [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) è configurato con un *startupTimeLimit* predefinito di 120 secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-592">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-593">Quando si mantiene il valore predefinito, l'avvio di un'app potrebbe richiedere fino a due minuti prima che il modulo registri un errore del processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-593">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-594">Per informazioni sulla configurazione del modulo, vedere [Attributi dell'elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-594">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-595">Risolvere i problemi nel servizio app di AzureTroubleshoot on Azure App Service</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-595">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-596">Registro eventi applicazioni (servizio app di Azure)Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-596">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-597">Per accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione, usare il pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-597">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-598">Nel portale di Azure aprire l'app in **Servizi app**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-598">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-599">Selezionare **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-599">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-600">Selezionare l'intestazione **Strumenti di diagnostica**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-600">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-601">In **Strumenti di supporto** selezionare il pulsante **Eventi dell'applicazione**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-601">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-602">Esaminare l'errore più recente dalla voce *IIS AspNetCoreModule* o *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* nella colonna **Origine**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-602">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-603">Un'alternativa all'uso del pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** consiste nell'esaminare direttamente il file del log eventi dell'applicazione usando [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-603">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-604">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-604">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-605">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-605">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-606">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-606">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-607">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-607">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-608">Aprire la cartella **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-608">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-609">Selezionare l'icona della matita accanto al file *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-609">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-610">Esaminare il log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-610">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-611">Scorrere fino alla fine del log per visualizzare gli eventi più recenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-611">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-612">Eseguire l'app nella console Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-612">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-613">Molti errori di avvio non producono informazioni utili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-613">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-614">È possibile eseguire l'app nella console di esecuzione remota [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) per individuare l'errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-614">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-615">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-615">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-616">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-616">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-617">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-617">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-618">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-618">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-619">Test di un'app a 32 bit (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-619">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-620">**Versione corrente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-620">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-621">Eseguire l'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-621">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-622">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-622">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-623">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-623">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-624">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-624">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-625">**Distribuzione dipendente dal framework in esecuzione in una versione di anteprima**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-625">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-626">*Richiede l'installazione dell'estensione del sito del runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-626">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-627">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` è la versione di runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-627">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-628">Eseguire l'app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-628">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-630">Test di un'app a 64 bit (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-630">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-631">**Versione corrente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-631">**Current release**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-632">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd) a 64 bit (x64):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-632">If the app is a 64-bit (x64) [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\Program Files\dotnet`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-633">Eseguire l'app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-633">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-634">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-634">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>
  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-636">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-636">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-637">**Distribuzione dipendente dal framework in esecuzione in una versione di anteprima**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-637">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-638">*Richiede l'installazione dell'estensione del sito del runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-638">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-639">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` è la versione di runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-639">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x64` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-640">Eseguire l'app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-640">Run the app: `dotnet \home\site\wwwroot\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-641">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà inviato alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-641">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-642">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-642">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-643">Il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core spesso registra utili messaggi di errore non disponibili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-643">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-644">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-644">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-645">Passare al pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-645">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-646">In **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY** (SELEZIONARE LA CATEGORIA DEL PROBLEMA) selezionare il pulsante **Web App Down** (App Web inattiva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-646">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-647">In \*\*Suggested Solutions (Soluzioni consigliate) \*\* > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection** (Abilita il reindirizzamento del log Stdout) selezionare il pulsante **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config** (Apri la console Kudu per modificare Web.Config).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-647">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-648">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-648">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-649">Scorrere verso il basso fino a visualizzare il file *web.config* in fondo all'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-649">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-650">Fare clic sull'icona della matita accanto al file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-650">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-651">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e cambiare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-651">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-652">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-652">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-653">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-653">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-654">Tornare al portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-654">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-655">Selezionare il pannello **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **STRUMENTI DI SVILUPPO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-655">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-656">Selezionare il pulsante **Vai&rarr;**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-656">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-657">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-657">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-658">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-658">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-659">Selezionare la cartella **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-659">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-660">Controllare la colonna **Data modifica** e selezionare l'icona della matita per modificare il log stdout con la data di modifica più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-660">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-661">Quando si apre il file di log, verrà visualizzato l'errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-661">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-662">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-662">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-663">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu tornare al percorso **site** > **wwwroot** per visualizzare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-663">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-664">Aprire nuovamente il file **web.config** selezionando l'icona della matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-664">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-665">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-665">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-666">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-666">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-667">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-667">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-668">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-668">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-669">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-669">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-670">Usare la registrazione stdout solo per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-670">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-671">Per la registrazione generale in un'app ASP.NET Core dopo l'avvio, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-671">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-672">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-672">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-673">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-673">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-674">Il log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core fornisce dati di registrazione aggiuntivi e più approfonditi dal modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-674">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-675">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-675">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

     1. <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-684">Aprire le cartelle al percorso > **wwwroot**. **site**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-684">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-685">Modificare il file *web.config* selezionando il pulsante a forma di matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-685">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-686">Aggiungere la sezione `<handlerSettings>` come illustrato in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-686">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c4df8-687">Fare clic sul pulsante **Salva**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-687">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="c4df8-707">App lenta o sporgente (servizio app di Azure)Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-707">Slow or hanging app (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c4df8-708">Quando un'app risponde lentamente o si blocca durante una richiesta, vedere gli articoli seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c4df8-708">When an app responds slowly or hangs on a request, see the following articles:</span></span>
